An Empirical Risk Minimization Approach for Offline Inverse RL and Dynamic Discrete Choice Model
Authors: Enoch H. Kang, Hema Yoganarasimhan, Lalit Jain
First: 2025-02-19T22:22:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T04:57:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study the problem of estimating Dynamic Discrete Choice (DDC) models, also known as offline Maximum Entropy-Regularized Inverse Reinforcement Learning (offline MaxEnt-IRL) in machine learning. The objective is to recover reward or $Q^*$ functions that govern agent behavior from offline behavior data. In this paper, we propose a globally convergent gradient-based method for solving these problems without the restrictive assumption of linearly parameterized rewards. The novelty of our approach lies in introducing the Empirical Risk Minimization (ERM) based IRL/DDC framework, which circumvents the need for explicit state transition probability estimation in the Bellman equation. Furthermore, our method is compatible with non-parametric estimation techniques such as neural networks. Therefore, the proposed method has the potential to be scaled to high-dimensional, infinite state spaces. A key theoretical insight underlying our approach is that the Bellman residual satisfies the Polyak-Lojasiewicz (PL) condition -- a property that, while weaker than strong convexity, is sufficient to ensure fast global convergence guarantees. Through a series of synthetic experiments, we demonstrate that our approach consistently outperforms benchmark methods and state-of-the-art alternatives.
中文标题/摘要
标题：离线逆强化学习与动态离散选择模型的经验风险最小化方法
本文研究动态离散选择（DDC）模型的估计问题，该问题在机器学习中也被称为离线最大熵正则化逆强化学习（offline MaxEnt-IRL）。目标是从离线行为数据中恢复支配智能体行为的奖励函数或$Q^*$函数。我们提出了一种全局收敛的梯度方法来解决这些问题，无需线性参数化奖励的严格假设。该方法的新颖之处在于引入了基于经验风险最小化（ERM）的IRL/DDC框架，从而避免了在贝尔曼方程中显式估计状态转移概率的需求。此外，我们的方法兼容神经网络等非参数估计技术，因此具有扩展到高维、无限状态空间的潜力。支撑该方法的关键理论洞见在于：贝尔曼残差满足Polyak-Lojasiewicz（PL）条件——该性质虽弱于强凸性，但足以确保快速全局收敛保证。通过一系列合成实验，我们证明该方法始终优于基准方法和现有最优替代方案。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the problem of estimating Dynamic Discrete Choice (DDC) models, also known as offline Maximum Entropy-Regularized Inverse Reinforcement Learning (offline MaxEnt-IRL), aiming to recover reward or Q* functions from offline behavior data. The authors propose a globally convergent gradient-based method that introduces an Empirical Risk Minimization (ERM) framework, which eliminates the need for explicit state transition probability estimation in the Bellman equation and is compatible with non-parametric techniques like neural networks, enabling scalability to high-dimensional infinite state spaces. The key theoretical insight is that the Bellman residual satisfies the Polyak-Lojasiewicz (PL) condition, ensuring fast global convergence, and synthetic experiments show the method consistently outperforms benchmark and state-of-the-art alternatives.

HiMAC: Hierarchical Macro-Micro Learning for Long-Horizon LLM Agents
Authors: Hongbo Jin, Rongpeng Zhu, Jiayu Ding, Guibo Luo, Ge Li
First: 2026-03-01T08:09:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T03:37:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) agents have recently demonstrated strong capabilities in interactive decision-making, yet they remain fundamentally limited in long-horizon tasks that require structured planning and reliable execution. Existing approaches predominantly rely on flat autoregressive policies, where high-level reasoning and low-level actions are generated within a single token sequence, leading to inefficient exploration and severe error propagation over extended trajectories. In this work, we propose HiMAC, a hierarchical agentic RL framework that explicitly decomposes long-horizon decision-making into macro-level planning and micro-level execution. HiMAC models reasoning as a structured blueprint generation process followed by goal-conditioned action execution, enabling robust long-horizon planning within LLM-based agents. To train this hierarchy efficiently, we introduce a critic-free hierarchical policy optimization paradigm that extends group-based reinforcement learning to bi-level structures through hierarchical relative advantage estimation. Furthermore, we propose an iterative co-evolution training strategy that alternates between planner exploration and executor adaptation, mitigating the non-stationarity inherent in hierarchical learning. Extensive experiments on ALFWorld, WebShop, and Sokoban demonstrate that HiMAC consistently outperforms strong prompting and reinforcement learning baselines, achieving state-of-the-art performance and substantially improved sample efficiency across both text-based and visually grounded environments. Our results show that introducing structured hierarchy, rather than increasing model scale alone, is a key factor for enabling robust long-horizon agentic intelligence.
DGPO: Distribution Guided Policy Optimization for Fine Grained Credit Assignment
Authors: Hongbo Jin, Rongpeng Zhu, Zhongjing Du, Xu Jiang, Jingqi Tian, Qiaoman Zhang, Jiayu Ding
First: 2026-05-05T03:36:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T03:36:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning is crucial for aligning large language models to perform complex reasoning tasks. However, current algorithms such as Group Relative Policy Optimization suffer from coarse grained, sequence level credit assignment, which severely struggles to isolate pivotal reasoning steps within long Chain of Thought generations. Furthermore, the standard unbounded Kullback Leibler divergence penalty induces severe gradient instability and mode seeking conservatism, ultimately stifling the discovery of novel reasoning trajectories. To overcome these limitations, we introduce Distribution Guided Policy Optimization, a novel critic free reinforcement learning framework that reinterprets distribution deviation as a guiding signal rather than a rigid penalty.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DGPO：面向细粒度信用分配的分布引导策略优化
强化学习对于对齐大型语言模型以执行复杂推理任务至关重要。然而，当前算法（如群体相对策略优化）存在粗粒度、序列级别的信用分配问题，难以在长链思维生成中隔离关键推理步骤。此外，标准无界KL散度惩罚会导致严重的梯度不稳定性和模式寻求保守性，最终抑制新推理轨迹的发现。为克服这些限制，我们提出分布引导策略优化，一种新颖的无评论家强化学习框架，将分布偏差重新解释为引导信号而非刚性惩罚。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Distribution Guided Policy Optimization (DGPO) to address coarse-grained credit assignment and gradient instability in reinforcement learning for large language models. DGPO replaces the standard unbounded KL divergence penalty with a guiding signal derived from distribution deviation, enabling fine-grained credit assignment at the step level. Experimental results demonstrate that DGPO significantly improves reasoning accuracy and exploration efficiency over Group Relative Policy Optimization on complex reasoning tasks.
该论文提出分布引导策略优化（DGPO），以解决强化学习在大语言模型中的粗粒度信用分配和梯度不稳定问题。DGPO将标准的无界KL散度惩罚替换为基于分布偏差的引导信号，实现步骤级别的细粒度信用分配。实验结果表明，在复杂推理任务上，DGPO相比组相对策略优化显著提升了推理准确率和探索效率。
Decoupled Guidance Diffusion for Adaptive Offline Safe Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Rufeng Chen, Zhaofan Zhang, Zhejiang Yang, Hechang Chen, Sihong Xie
First: 2026-05-04T16:19:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T02:44:52+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline safe reinforcement learning often requires policies to adapt at deployment time to safety budgets that vary across episodes or change within a single episode. While diffusion-based planners enable flexible trajectory generation, existing guidance schemes often treat reward improvement and constraint satisfaction as competing gradient objectives, which can lead to unreliable safety compliance under cost limits. We reinterpret adaptive safe trajectory generation as sampling from a constrained trajectory distribution, where the budget restricts the trajectory region, and reward shapes preferences within that region. This perspective motivates Safe Decoupled Guidance Diffusion (SDGD), which conditions classifier-free guidance on the cost limit to bias sampling toward trajectories satisfying the specified limit, while using reward-gradient guidance to refine trajectories for higher return. Because direct reward guidance can increase return while also steering samples toward trajectories with higher cumulative cost, we introduce Feasible Trajectory Relabeling (FTR) to reshape reward targets and discourage such directions. We further provide a first-order sampling-time analysis showing that FTR suppresses reward-induced cost drift under a prefix-restorative alignment condition. Extensive evaluations on the DSRL benchmark show that SDGD achieves the strongest safety compliance among baselines, satisfying the constraint on 94.7% of tasks (36/38), while obtaining the highest reward among safe methods on 21 tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：解耦引导扩散用于自适应离线安全强化学习
离线安全强化学习通常要求策略在部署时能够适应跨回合变化或单回合内变化的安全预算。虽然基于扩散的规划器能够实现灵活的轨迹生成，但现有的引导方案往往将奖励提升和约束满足视为竞争性的梯度目标，这可能导致在成本限制下安全合规性不可靠。我们将自适应安全轨迹生成重新解释为从受约束的轨迹分布中采样，其中预算限制了轨迹区域，而奖励则在该区域内塑造偏好。这一视角催生了安全解耦引导扩散（SDGD），该方法将无分类器引导条件化为成本限制，以将采样偏向于满足指定限制的轨迹，同时使用奖励梯度引导来优化轨迹以获得更高回报。由于直接的奖励引导可能增加回报，同时也会将样本引向累积成本更高的轨迹，我们引入了可行轨迹重标记（FTR）来重塑奖励目标并抑制此类方向。我们进一步提供了一阶采样时间分析，表明在前缀恢复对齐条件下，FTR抑制了奖励引起的成本漂移。在DSRL基准上的广泛评估显示，SDGD在基线中实现了最强的安全合规性，在94.7%的任务（36/38）上满足约束，同时在21个任务上获得了安全方法中的最高奖励。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of offline safe reinforcement learning where policies must adapt to varying safety budgets at deployment time. The authors propose Safe Decoupled Guidance Diffusion (SDGD), which reinterprets adaptive safe trajectory generation as sampling from a constrained trajectory distribution, using classifier-free guidance conditioned on cost limits to ensure safety compliance and reward-gradient guidance to maximize returns. To prevent reward guidance from increasing cumulative costs, they introduce Feasible Trajectory Relabeling (FTR) to reshape reward targets, supported by a first-order sampling-time analysis showing FTR suppresses cost drift. Experiments on the DSRL benchmark demonstrate that SDGD achieves the strongest safety compliance, satisfying constraints on 94.7% of tasks (36/38) while obtaining the highest reward among safe methods on 21 tasks.
该论文针对离线安全强化学习中策略需在部署时适应变化安全预算的问题。作者提出安全解耦引导扩散（SDGD），将自适应安全轨迹生成重新解释为从受约束轨迹分布中采样，利用基于成本限制的无分类器引导确保安全合规，并使用奖励梯度引导最大化回报。为防止奖励引导增加累积成本，他们引入可行轨迹重标记（FTR）重塑奖励目标，并通过一阶采样时间分析证明FTR能抑制成本漂移。在DSRL基准上的实验表明，SDGD实现了最强的安全合规性，在94.7%的任务（36/38）上满足约束，同时在21个任务上获得了安全方法中的最高奖励。
Learn where to Click from Yourself: On-Policy Self-Distillation for GUI Grounding
Authors: Yan Zhang, Daiqing Wu, Huawen Shen, Yu Zhou, Can Ma
First: 2026-05-01T13:23:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T01:14:44+00:00
Comments: under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Graphical User Interface (GUI) grounding maps natural language instructions to the visual coordinates of target elements and serves as a core capability for autonomous GUI agents. Recent reinforcement learning methods (e.g., GRPO) have achieved strong performance, but they rely on expensive multiple rollouts and suffer from sparse signals on hard samples. These limitations make on-policy self-distillation (OPSD), which provides dense token-level supervision from a single rollout, a promising alternative. However, its applicability to GUI grounding remains unexplored. In this paper, we present GUI-SD, the first OPSD framework tailored for GUI grounding. First, it constructs a visually enriched privileged context for the teacher using a target bounding box and a Gaussian soft mask, providing informative guidance without leaking exact coordinates. Second, it employs entropy-guided distillation, which adaptively weights tokens based on digit significance and teacher confidence, concentrating optimization on the most impactful and reliable positions. Extensive experiments on six representative GUI grounding benchmarks show that GUI-SD consistently outperforms GRPO-based methods and naive OPSD in both accuracy and training efficiency. Code and training data are available at https://zhangyan-ucas.github.io/GUI-SD/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从自身学习点击位置：面向GUI定位的在线策略自蒸馏方法
图形用户界面（GUI）定位将自然语言指令映射到目标元素的视觉坐标，是自主GUI智能体的核心能力。近期强化学习方法（如GRPO）取得了强劲性能，但依赖昂贵的多次展开，且在困难样本上存在稀疏信号问题。这些局限使得在线策略自蒸馏（OPSD）成为有前景的替代方案——它通过单次展开提供密集的令牌级监督。然而，其适用于GUI定位的可行性尚未被探索。本文提出GUI-SD，首个专为GUI定位设计的OPSD框架。首先，它利用目标边界框和高斯软掩码为教师构建视觉增强的特权上下文，在不泄露精确坐标的前提下提供信息性指导。其次，采用熵引导蒸馏，根据数字重要性和教师置信度自适应加权令牌，将优化聚焦于最具影响力和可靠的位置。在六个代表性GUI定位基准上的大量实验表明，GUI-SD在准确率和训练效率上均持续优于基于GRPO的方法和朴素OPSD。代码和训练数据见https://zhangyan-ucas.github.io/GUI-SD/。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces GUI-SD, the first on-policy self-distillation (OPSD) framework for GUI grounding, motivated by the limitations of reinforcement learning methods like GRPO that require expensive multiple rollouts and provide sparse signals on hard samples. The method constructs a visually enriched privileged context for the teacher using a target bounding box and Gaussian soft mask, then applies entropy-guided distillation to adaptively weight tokens based on digit significance and teacher confidence. Extensive experiments on six GUI grounding benchmarks demonstrate that GUI-SD consistently outperforms GRPO-based methods and naive OPSD in both accuracy and training efficiency.
本文提出GUI-SD，首个针对GUI定位的在线自蒸馏框架，其动机在于克服强化学习方法（如GRPO）需要多次采样且对困难样本信号稀疏的局限。该方法通过目标边界框和高斯软掩码为教师模型构建视觉增强特权上下文，并采用熵引导蒸馏，根据数字重要性和教师置信度自适应调整令牌权重。在六个GUI定位基准上的大量实验表明，GUI-SD在准确率和训练效率上均持续优于基于GRPO的方法和朴素在线自蒸馏方法。
Taking the GP Out of the Loop
Authors: Mehul Bafna, Siddhant anand Jadhav, David Sweet
First: 2025-06-15T11:37:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T00:20:54+00:00
Comments: 21 pages, 17 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bayesian optimization (BO) has traditionally solved black-box problems where function evaluation is expensive and, therefore, observations are few. Recently, however, there has been growing interest in applying BO to problems where function evaluation is cheaper and observations are more plentiful. In this regime, scaling to many observations $N$ is impeded by Gaussian-process (GP) surrogates: GP hyperparameter fitting scales as $\mathcal{O}(N^3)$ (reduced to roughly $\mathcal{O}(N^2)$ in modern implementations), and it is repeated at every BO iteration. Many methods improve scaling at acquisition time, but hyperparameter fitting still scales poorly, making it the bottleneck. We propose Epistemic Nearest Neighbors (ENN), a lightweight alternative to GPs that estimates function values and uncertainty (epistemic and aleatoric) from $K$-nearest-neighbor observations. ENN scales as $\mathcal{O}(N)$ for both fitting and acquisition. Our BO method, TuRBO-ENN, replaces the GP surrogate in TuRBO with ENN and its Thompson-sampling acquisition with $\mathrm{UCB} = μ(x) + σ(x)$. For the special case of noise-free problems, we can omit fitting altogether by replacing $\mathrm{UCB}$ with a non-dominated sort over $μ(x)$ and $σ(x)$. We show empirically that TuRBO-ENN reduces proposal time (i.e., fitting time + acquisition time) by one to two orders of magnitude compared to TuRBO at up to 50,000 observations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：将高斯过程从循环中移除
贝叶斯优化（BO）传统上用于解决函数评估成本高昂、观测数据稀少的黑箱问题。然而，近年来，人们越来越关注将BO应用于函数评估成本较低、观测数据更丰富的问题。在此场景下，扩展到大量观测数据$N$受到高斯过程（GP）代理模型的阻碍：GP超参数拟合的复杂度为$\mathcal{O}(N^3)$（在现代实现中降至约$\mathcal{O}(N^2)$），且每次BO迭代都需要重复进行。许多方法在采集阶段改善了扩展性，但超参数拟合的扩展性仍然很差，成为瓶颈。我们提出了一种轻量级的GP替代方法——认知最近邻（ENN），它通过$K$近邻观测来估计函数值和不确定性（认知性和偶然性）。ENN在拟合和采集阶段的复杂度均为$\mathcal{O}(N)$。我们的BO方法TuRBO-ENN将TuRBO中的GP代理替换为ENN，并将其汤普森采样采集函数替换为$\mathrm{UCB} = μ(x) + σ(x)$。对于无噪声问题的特殊情况，我们可以通过用$μ(x)$和$σ(x)$的非支配排序替换$\mathrm{UCB}$来完全省略拟合过程。实验表明，在多达50,000个观测数据的情况下，与TuRBO相比，TuRBO-ENN将提议时间（即拟合时间+采集时间）减少了一到两个数量级。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the scalability bottleneck of Gaussian process (GP) surrogates in Bayesian optimization (BO) when function evaluations are cheap and observations are plentiful, as GP hyperparameter fitting scales poorly (O(N^3) to O(N^2)). The authors propose Epistemic Nearest Neighbors (ENN), a lightweight method that estimates function values and uncertainty from K-nearest-neighbor observations, scaling as O(N) for both fitting and acquisition. Their BO method, TuRBO-ENN, replaces the GP surrogate with ENN and uses UCB acquisition, or a non-dominated sort for noise-free problems. Experimental results show that TuRBO-ENN reduces proposal time (fitting plus acquisition) by one to two orders of magnitude compared to TuRBO at up to 50,000 observations.
该论文针对贝叶斯优化中，当函数评估成本低且观测数据多时，高斯过程代理模型因超参数拟合复杂度高（O(N^3)至O(N^2)）而成为瓶颈的问题。作者提出了轻量级的近邻认知不确定性方法，通过K近邻观测估计函数值和不确定性，拟合与采集复杂度均为O(N)。其提出的TuRBO-ENN方法用ENN替代高斯过程代理，并采用UCB采集函数，对于无噪声问题则使用非支配排序。实验结果表明，在多达50,000个观测数据时，TuRBO-ENN相比TuRBO将提议时间（拟合加采集）降低了一到两个数量级。
The Hive Mind is a Single Reinforcement Learning Agent
Authors: Karthik Soma, Yann Bouteiller, Heiko Hamann, Giovanni Beltrame
First: 2024-10-23T02:49:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T22:46:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Decision-making is an essential attribute of any intelligent agent or group. Natural systems are known to converge to effective strategies through at least two distinct mechanisms: collective decision-making via imitation of others, and trial-and-error by a single agent. This paper establishes an equivalence between these two paradigms by drawing from the well-studied collective decision-making problem of nest-hunting in swarms of honey bees. We show that the emergent distributed cognition (sometimes referred to as the $\textit{hive mind}$) arising from individuals following simple, local imitation-based rules is that of a single online reinforcement learning (RL) agent interacting with many parallel environments. More specifically, in the purely imitative $\textit{weighted voter}$ model of bees' waggle dance, the update rule through which this macro-agent learns is a multi-armed bandit algorithm that we coin $\textit{Maynard-Cross Learning}$. Our analysis implies that a group of purely imitative organisms can be equivalent to a more complex, reinforcement-enabled entity, substantiating the idea that group-level intelligence may explain how seemingly simple and blind individual behaviors are selected in nature. Beyond biology, the framework offers new tools for analyzing economic and social systems where individuals imitate successful strategies, effectively participating in a collective learning process. Our findings may further inform the design of scalable RL-inspired collective systems in artificial domains.
Summary / 总结
This paper establishes an equivalence between collective decision-making via imitation and single-agent reinforcement learning, motivated by the nest-hunting behavior of honey bee swarms. The authors show that the emergent hive mind from individuals following local imitation rules corresponds to a single online RL agent interacting with parallel environments, where the update rule in the weighted voter model of waggle dances is a multi-armed bandit algorithm called Maynard-Cross Learning. The analysis demonstrates that a group of purely imitative organisms can function as a reinforcement-enabled entity, providing new tools for analyzing social and economic systems and informing the design of scalable RL-inspired collective systems.
本文受蜜蜂蜂群巢穴搜寻行为的启发，建立了通过模仿进行集体决策与单智能体强化学习之间的等价关系。作者证明，个体遵循局部模仿规则所涌现出的蜂群思维对应于一个与多个并行环境交互的在线强化学习智能体，其中在蜜蜂摇摆舞的加权投票者模型中，更新规则是一种名为梅纳德-克罗斯学习的多臂老虎机算法。分析表明，纯粹模仿的群体可以等同于一个具备强化能力的实体，为分析经济和社会系统提供了新工具，并为设计可扩展的类强化学习集体系统提供了启示。
Terminus-4B: Can a Smaller Model Replace Frontier LLMs at Agentic Execution Tasks?
Authors: Spandan Garg, Vikram Nitin, Yufan Huang
First: 2026-05-04T22:24:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T22:24:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern coding agents increasingly delegate specialized subtasks to subagents, which are smaller, focused agentic loops that handle narrow responsibilities like search, debugging or terminal execution. This architectural pattern keeps the main agent's context window clean by isolating verbose outputs (e.g. build logs, test results, etc.) within the subagent context. Typically when agents employ subagents for such tasks, they use frontier models as these subagents. In this paper, we investigate whether a finetuned small language model (SLM) can achieve comparable performance to frontier models in the task of agentic terminal execution. We present Terminus-4B, which is a post-trained Qwen3-4B model via Supervised Finetuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL) using rubric-based LLM-as-judge reward, specifically for this task. In our extensive evaluation spanning various frontier models, training ablations and main agent configurations, we find that Terminus-4B is able to reduce the token usage of the main agent by up to ~30% compared to the No Subagent baseline with no impact to agent performance on benchmarks like SWE-Bench Pro and our internal SWE-Bench C# benchmark, which tends to be heavy in verbose execution tasks. Furthermore, Terminus-4B improves key metrics showing the main agent relying on the outputs of the subagent and doing fewer terminal execution tasks by itself. We see that our model not only closes the gap between the Vanilla Qwen model and frontier models like Claude Sonnet / Opus / GPT-5.3-Codex, but often even exceeds their performance.
Summary / 总结
The paper investigates whether a small finetuned language model can replace frontier models as subagents for agentic terminal execution tasks, motivated by the need to reduce token usage and keep main agent context windows clean. The authors present Terminus-4B, a post-trained Qwen3-4B model using supervised finetuning and reinforcement learning with a rubric-based LLM-as-judge reward. Experimental results on SWE-Bench Pro and an internal C# benchmark show that Terminus-4B reduces main agent token usage by up to 30% compared to a no-subagent baseline without harming performance, and often exceeds the performance of frontier models like Claude Sonnet, Opus, and GPT-5.3-Codex.
本文研究小型微调语言模型能否替代前沿模型作为子代理执行终端任务，动机是减少令牌使用并保持主代理上下文窗口清洁。作者提出Terminus-4B，基于Qwen3-4B模型，通过监督微调和基于评分标准的LLM作为评判奖励的强化学习进行后训练。在SWE-Bench Pro和内部C#基准测试上的实验结果显示，Terminus-4B相比无子代理基线将主代理令牌使用量减少高达30%，且不影响性能，并常超越Claude Sonnet、Opus和GPT-5.3-Codex等前沿模型的表现。
Bootstrapped Mixed Rewards for RL Post-Training: Injecting Canonical Action Order
Authors: Prakhar Gupta, Vaibhav Gupta
First: 2025-12-03T21:36:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T21:36:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Post-training with reinforcement learning (RL) typically optimizes a single scalar objective and ignores structure in how solutions are produced. We ask whether a scalar hint toward a canonical solver ordering, used only during RL post-training, improves performance even when fine-tuned on randomized solution sequences. On Zebra puzzles, we fine-tune a Transformer on randomized solution orders, then post-train it with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) using two rewards: a sparse task reward that is 1 only when the puzzle is fully solved, and an ordering reward that increases when the model's emission order aligns with the canonical solver order. To compare signals cleanly, we combine them via fixed mixtures and use a simple bootstrapped scaling to equalize component magnitudes at initialization. Mixed rewards generally outperform task-only optimization, suggesting that coarse ordering signals can steer RL post-training toward canonical trajectories without modifying supervised data or architecture.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自举混合奖励用于强化学习后训练：注入规范动作顺序
强化学习后训练通常优化单一标量目标，忽略解决方案生成的结构。我们探究在RL后训练期间仅使用指向规范求解器顺序的标量提示，是否能在随机化解决方案序列上微调时提升性能。在斑马谜题中，我们在随机化解法顺序上微调Transformer，然后使用组相对策略优化（GRPO）进行后训练，采用两种奖励：稀疏任务奖励（仅当谜题完全解决时为1）和排序奖励（当模型输出顺序与规范求解器顺序一致时增加）。为清晰比较信号，我们通过固定混合组合它们，并使用简单的自举缩放来在初始化时均衡各分量幅度。混合奖励通常优于仅任务优化，表明粗略的排序信号可以引导RL后训练走向规范轨迹，而无需修改监督数据或架构。
Summary / 总结
The paper investigates whether injecting a canonical action ordering signal during reinforcement learning (RL) post-training can improve model performance even when fine-tuned on randomized solution sequences. The authors propose a method that combines a sparse task reward (1 only when fully solved) with an ordering reward that increases when the model's emission order aligns with a canonical solver order, using fixed mixtures and bootstrapped scaling to balance component magnitudes. Applied to Zebra puzzles with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), mixed rewards consistently outperform task-only optimization, demonstrating that coarse ordering signals can steer RL post-training toward canonical trajectories without altering supervised data or architecture.
该论文探讨了在强化学习后训练中注入规范动作排序信号是否能在微调随机解序列时提升模型性能。作者提出了一种方法，将稀疏任务奖励（仅在完全解谜时为1）与排序奖励（当模型输出顺序与规范求解器顺序一致时增加）结合，通过固定混合和自举缩放平衡各分量幅度。在斑马谜题上使用组相对策略优化（GRPO）进行实验，混合奖励始终优于仅任务优化，表明粗略的排序信号可以引导强化学习后训练走向规范轨迹，而无需修改监督数据或架构。
Robust Differential Evolution via Nonlinear Population Size Reduction and Adaptive Restart: The ARRDE Algorithm
Authors: Khoirul Faiq Muzakka, Ahsani Hafizhu Shali, Haris Suhendar, Sören Möller, Martin Finsterbusch
First: 2025-11-23T12:50:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T21:19:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This study is motivated by a robustness issue in numerical optimization of bound-constrained problems: many algorithms that perform well on a particular benchmark suite, such as the IEEE CEC2017 problems, struggle to maintain the same level of performance when applied to other suites that differ in dimensionality, landscape complexity, or the maximum number of function evaluations ($N_{\text{max}}$). To address this issue, we propose the Adaptive Restart--Refine Differential Evolution (ARRDE) algorithm, a variant of Differential Evolution (DE) built on jSO. ARRDE is centered on two main design contributions: an adaptive restart--refine mechanism, which includes final-stage refinement and local exclusion during restart, and a nonlinear population-size reduction strategy whose shape depends on problem dimensionality. We evaluate ARRDE on five benchmark suites: CEC2011, CEC2017, CEC2019, CEC2020, and CEC2022. To the best of our knowledge, this is one of the most comprehensive experimental studies conducted in this context. Because the official metrics of these benchmark suites emphasize different performance aspects, we additionally introduce a bounded accuracy-based scoring metric derived from relative error for cross-suite robustness assessment. Using both the official suite-specific metrics and the proposed robustness-oriented metric, ARRDE consistently demonstrates top-tier performance and one of the most stable aggregate profiles across all benchmark suites. These results support ARRDE as a competitive and robust DE variant across heterogeneous benchmark regimes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于非线性种群规模缩减与自适应重启的鲁棒差分进化：ARRDE算法
本研究源于边界约束问题数值优化中的鲁棒性挑战：许多在特定基准测试集（如IEEE CEC2017问题）上表现优异的算法，在应用于维度、景观复杂度或最大函数评估次数（$N_{\text{max}}$）不同的其他测试集时，难以维持同等性能水平。为此，我们提出自适应重启-精炼差分进化（ARRDE）算法，这是基于jSO构建的差分进化（DE）变体。ARRDE的核心包含两项主要设计贡献：自适应重启-精炼机制（包括最终阶段精炼和重启时的局部排除），以及形状取决于问题维度的非线性种群规模缩减策略。 我们在五个基准测试集上评估ARRDE：CEC2011、CEC2017、CEC2019、CEC2020和CEC2022。据我们所知，这是该领域最全面的实验研究之一。由于这些基准测试集的官方指标侧重不同性能维度，我们额外引入基于相对误差的有界精度评分指标，用于跨测试集的鲁棒性评估。结合官方特定测试集指标与所提出的鲁棒性导向指标，ARRDE在所有基准测试集中持续展现顶级性能与最稳定的聚合轮廓之一。这些结果支持ARRDE作为跨异构基准测试体系具有竞争力和鲁棒性的DE变体。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the robustness issue where algorithms excelling on one benchmark suite (e.g., CEC2017) often fail to maintain performance across suites with varying dimensionality, landscape complexity, or evaluation budgets, this paper proposes the Adaptive Restart–Refine Differential Evolution (ARRDE) algorithm. Built on jSO, ARRDE introduces two key innovations: an adaptive restart–refine mechanism with final-stage refinement and local exclusion during restart, and a nonlinear population-size reduction strategy shaped by problem dimensionality. Evaluated on five benchmark suites (CEC2011, CEC2017, CEC2019, CEC2020, CEC2022) using both official metrics and a novel bounded accuracy-based scoring metric for cross-suite robustness, ARRDE consistently achieves top-tier performance and the most stable aggregate profiles, establishing it as a competitive and robust DE variant across heterogeneous optimization regimes.
针对许多算法在特定基准套件（如CEC2017）上表现优异，但在维度、景观复杂度或最大函数评估次数不同的其他套件上性能下降的鲁棒性问题，本文提出了自适应重启-细化差分进化（ARRDE）算法。该算法基于jSO构建，核心创新包括：自适应重启-细化机制（含最终阶段细化和重启时的局部排除），以及依赖问题维度的非线性种群规模缩减策略。在CEC2011、CEC2017、CEC2019、CEC2020和CEC2022五个基准套件上，使用官方指标和新增的基于相对误差的有界精度评分指标进行跨套件鲁棒性评估，ARRDE始终表现出顶尖性能和最稳定的聚合轮廓，被证实为一种在异构优化场景中具有竞争力和鲁棒性的DE变体。
Transformer-Guided Deep Reinforcement Learning for Optimal Takeoff Trajectory Design of an eVTOL Drone
Authors: Nathan M. Roberts, Xiaosong Du
First: 2025-11-18T20:11:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T21:14:49+00:00
Comments: Conference version with 12 pages and 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid advancement of electric vertical takeoff and landing (eVTOL) aircraft offers a promising opportunity to alleviate urban traffic congestion but is still limited by excessive power demands, especially during the takeoff phase. Thus, developing optimal takeoff trajectories for minimum energy consumption becomes essential for broader eVTOL aircraft applications. Conventional optimal control methods (such as dynamic programming and linear quadratic regulator) provide highly efficient and well-established solutions but are prohibited by problem dimensionality and complexity. Deep reinforcement learning (DRL) emerges as a special type of artificial intelligence tackling complex, nonlinear systems; however, the training difficulty is a key bottleneck that hinders DRL applications. To address these challenges, we propose the transformer-guided DRL to alleviate the training difficulty by exploring a realistic state space at each time step using a transformer. The proposed transformer-guided DRL was demonstrated on an optimal takeoff trajectory design of an eVTOL drone for minimal energy consumption while meeting takeoff conditions (i.e., minimum vertical displacement and minimum horizontal velocity) by varying control variables (i.e., power and wing angle to the vertical). Results presented that the transformer-guided DRL agent learned to take off with $4.57\times10^6$ time steps, representing $25\%$ of the $19.79\times10^6$ time steps needed by a vanilla DRL agent. In addition, the transformer-guided DRL achieved $97.2\%$ accuracy on the optimal energy consumption compared against the simulation-based optimal reference, while the vanilla DRL achieved $96.1\%$ accuracy. Therefore, the proposed transformer-guided DRL outperformed vanilla DRL in terms of both training efficiency and optimal design verification.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于Transformer引导的深度强化学习用于eVTOL无人机最优起飞轨迹设计
电动垂直起降（eVTOL）飞行器的快速发展为缓解城市交通拥堵提供了有前景的机遇，但仍受限于过高的功率需求，尤其是在起飞阶段。因此，开发最小能耗的最优起飞轨迹对于eVTOL飞行器的广泛应用至关重要。传统最优控制方法（如动态规划和线性二次型调节器）提供了高效且成熟的解决方案，但受限于问题维度和复杂性。深度强化学习（DRL）作为一种特殊的人工智能方法，能够处理复杂的非线性系统；然而，训练难度是阻碍DRL应用的关键瓶颈。为应对这些挑战，我们提出了Transformer引导的DRL，通过在每个时间步利用Transformer探索真实状态空间来缓解训练难度。所提出的Transformer引导DRL在eVTOL无人机最小能耗最优起飞轨迹设计中得到验证，通过改变控制变量（即功率和机翼与垂直方向的夹角）满足起飞条件（即最小垂直位移和最小水平速度）。结果表明，Transformer引导的DRL智能体在4.57×10^6时间步内学会起飞，仅为普通DRL智能体所需19.79×10^6时间步的25%。此外，与基于仿真的最优参考相比，Transformer引导的DRL在最优能耗上达到97.2%的准确率，而普通DRL达到96.1%的准确率。因此，所提出的Transformer引导DRL在训练效率和最优设计验证方面均优于普通DRL。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of high energy consumption during the takeoff phase of eVTOL drones by proposing a transformer-guided deep reinforcement learning (DRL) method to design optimal takeoff trajectories. The method integrates a transformer to explore a realistic state space at each time step, thereby alleviating the training difficulty inherent in vanilla DRL. Experimental results demonstrate that the transformer-guided DRL agent requires only 4.57 million time steps to learn, which is 25% of the 19.79 million steps needed by vanilla DRL, while achieving 97.2% accuracy on optimal energy consumption compared to a simulation-based reference, outperforming vanilla DRL's 96.1% accuracy.

A Unified Framework for Tabular Generative Modeling: Loss Functions, Benchmarks, and Improved Multi-objective Bayesian Optimization Approaches
Authors: Minh H. Vu, Daniel Edler, Carl Wibom, Tommy Löfstedt, Beatrice Melin, Martin Rosvall
Venue: Transactions on Machine Learning Research (TMLR), 2026. https://openreview.net/forum?id=RPZ0EW0lz0
First: 2024-05-27T09:08:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T21:01:58+00:00
Comments: Published in Transactions on Machine Learning Research (TMLR), 2026. Code available at https://github.com/vuhoangminh/TabGen-Framework
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Deep learning (DL) models require extensive data to achieve strong performance and generalization. Deep generative models (DGMs) offer a solution by synthesizing data. Yet current approaches for tabular data often fail to preserve feature correlations and distributions during training, struggle with multi-metric hyperparameter selection, and lack comprehensive evaluation protocols. We address this gap with a unified framework that integrates training, hyperparameter tuning, and evaluation. First, we introduce a novel correlation- and distribution-aware loss function that regularizes DGMs, enhancing their ability to generate synthetic tabular data that faithfully represents the underlying data distributions. Theoretical analysis establishes stability and consistency guarantees. To enable principled hyperparameter search via Bayesian optimization (BO), we also propose a new multi-objective aggregation strategy based on iterative objective refinement Bayesian optimization (IORBO), along with a comprehensive statistical testing framework. We validate the proposed approach using a benchmarking framework with twenty real-world datasets and ten established tabular DGM baselines. The correlation-aware loss function significantly improves synthetic data fidelity and downstream machine learning (ML) performance, while IORBO consistently outperforms standard Bayesian optimization (SBO) in hyperparameter selection. The unified framework advances tabular generative modeling beyond isolated method improvements. Code is available at: https://github.com/vuhoangminh/TabGen-Framework
中文标题/摘要
标题：表格数据生成建模的统一框架：损失函数、基准测试与改进的多目标贝叶斯优化方法
深度学习模型需要大量数据才能实现强性能和泛化能力。深度生成模型通过合成数据提供了一种解决方案。然而，当前针对表格数据的方法在训练过程中往往无法保留特征相关性和分布，在多指标超参数选择上存在困难，且缺乏全面的评估协议。我们通过一个集成训练、超参数调优和评估的统一框架来填补这一空白。首先，我们引入了一种新颖的相关性与分布感知损失函数，用于正则化深度生成模型，增强其生成忠实代表底层数据分布的合成表格数据的能力。理论分析确立了稳定性和一致性保证。为了实现基于贝叶斯优化的原则性超参数搜索，我们还提出了一种基于迭代目标细化贝叶斯优化的新多目标聚合策略，并配套了全面的统计检验框架。我们使用包含二十个真实世界数据集和十个已建立表格深度生成模型基线的基准测试框架验证了所提方法。相关性感知损失函数显著提升了合成数据的保真度和下游机器学习性能，而迭代目标细化贝叶斯优化在超参数选择上始终优于标准贝叶斯优化。该统一框架将表格生成建模推进到超越孤立方法改进的层面。代码可在 https://github.com/vuhoangminh/TabGen-Framework 获取。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenges of deep generative models for tabular data, including poor preservation of feature correlations and distributions, difficulty in multi-metric hyperparameter selection, and lack of comprehensive evaluation protocols. The authors propose a unified framework integrating training, hyperparameter tuning, and evaluation, featuring a novel correlation- and distribution-aware loss function with theoretical stability and consistency guarantees, and a new multi-objective Bayesian optimization strategy called IORBO for principled hyperparameter search. Experiments on twenty real-world datasets with ten baselines show that the correlation-aware loss significantly improves synthetic data fidelity and downstream ML performance, while IORBO consistently outperforms standard Bayesian optimization in hyperparameter selection.
本文针对表格数据深度生成模型在训练中难以保持特征相关性和分布、多指标超参数选择困难以及缺乏全面评估协议的问题，提出了一个集成训练、超参数调优和评估的统一框架。该框架引入了一种新颖的相关性与分布感知损失函数，具有理论上的稳定性和一致性保证，并基于迭代目标细化贝叶斯优化（IORBO）提出了一种新的多目标聚合策略，用于实现原则性的超参数搜索。在二十个真实数据集和十个基线模型上的实验表明，相关性感知损失函数显著提升了合成数据的保真度和下游机器学习性能，而IORBO在超参数选择上持续优于标准贝叶斯优化。
Taming the Curses of Multiagency in Robust Markov Games with Large State Space through Linear Function Approximation
Authors: Jingchu Gai, Laixi Shi
First: 2026-05-04T20:04:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T20:04:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) holds great potential but faces robustness challenges due to environmental uncertainty. To address this, distributionally robust Markov games (RMGs) optimize worst-case performance when the environment deviates from the nominal model within a uncertainty set. Beyond robustness, an equally urgent goal for MARL is data efficiency -- sampling from vast state and action spaces that grow exponentially with the number of agents potentially leads to the curse of multiagency. However, current provably data-efficient algorithms for RMGs are limited to tabular settings with finite state and action spaces, which are only computationally manageable for small-scale problems, leaving RMGs with large-scale (or infinite) state spaces largely unexplored. The only existing work beyond tabular settings focuses on linear function approximation (LFA) for a restrictive class of RMGs using vanish minimal value assumption and still suffers from sample complexity with the curse of multiagency. In this work, we focuses on general RMGs with LFA. For uncertainty sets defined by total variation distance, we develop provably data-efficient algorithms that break the curse of multiagency in both the generative model setting and a newly proposed online interactive setting. To our knowledge, our results are the first to break the curse of multiagency of sample complexity for RMGs with large (possibly infinite) state spaces, regardless of the uncertainty set construction.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过线性函数逼近驯服大规模状态空间鲁棒马尔可夫博弈中的多智能体诅咒
多智能体强化学习（MARL）潜力巨大，但因环境不确定性面临鲁棒性挑战。为此，分布鲁棒马尔可夫博弈（RMG）在环境偏离名义模型且处于不确定集内时优化最坏情况性能。除鲁棒性外，MARL同样迫切的目标是数据效率——从随智能体数量指数增长的大规模状态与动作空间中采样可能导致多智能体诅咒。然而，当前RMG的可证明数据高效算法仅限于有限状态与动作空间的表格设置，仅能处理小规模问题，使得大规模（或无限）状态空间的RMG基本未被探索。唯一超越表格设置的现有工作聚焦于一类受限RMG的线性函数逼近（LFA），采用消失最小化值假设，且样本复杂度仍受多智能体诅咒影响。本文研究一般RMG的LFA。针对由总变差距离定义的不确定集，我们开发了可证明数据高效的算法，在生成模型设置和新提出的在线交互设置中均打破了多智能体诅咒。据我们所知，无论不确定集如何构造，我们的结果是首个打破大规模（可能无限）状态空间RMG样本复杂度中多智能体诅咒的工作。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the dual challenges of robustness and data efficiency in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) with large state spaces, where existing algorithms for distributionally robust Markov games (RMGs) suffer from the curse of multiagency and are limited to tabular settings. The authors propose provably data-efficient algorithms using linear function approximation (LFA) for general RMGs with uncertainty sets defined by total variation distance, covering both generative model and online interactive settings. Their main experimental results demonstrate that these algorithms break the curse of multiagency in sample complexity, achieving the first such results for RMGs with large or infinite state spaces regardless of uncertainty set construction.
该论文针对多智能体强化学习中大规模状态空间下的鲁棒性和数据效率双重挑战，现有分布鲁棒马尔可夫博弈算法受限于表格型设置且面临多智能体维数灾难。作者提出基于线性函数逼近的可证明数据高效算法，适用于总变差距离定义的不确定集，涵盖生成模型和在线交互两种场景。主要实验结果表明，这些算法在样本复杂度上突破了多智能体维数灾难，首次实现了对大规模或无限状态空间下分布鲁棒马尔可夫博弈的这一突破，且不依赖于不确定集的具体构造方式。
Optimal control of the future via prospective learning with control
Authors: Yuxin Bai, Aranyak Acharyya, Ashwin De Silva, Zeyu Shen, James Hassett, Joshua T. Vogelstein
First: 2025-11-11T19:27:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T18:26:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Optimal control of the future is the next frontier for AI. Current approaches to this problem are typically rooted in reinforcement learning (RL). RL is mathematically distinct from supervised learning, which has been the main workhorse for the recent achievements in AI. Moreover, RL typically operates in a stationary environment with episodic resets, limiting its utility. Here, we extend supervised learning to address learning to control in non-stationary, reset-free environments. Using this framework, called ''Prospective Learning with Control'' (PLuC), we prove that under certain fairly general assumptions, empirical risk minimization (ERM) asymptotically achieves the Bayes optimal policy. We then consider a specific instance of prospective learning with control: foraging, a canonical task relevant to both natural and artificial agents. We illustrate that modern RL algorithms, which assume stationarity, struggle in these non-stationary reset-free environments. Even with time-aware modifications, they converge orders of magnitude slower than our prospective foraging agents on a simple 1-D foraging benchmark. Code is available at: https://github.com/neurodata/procontrol.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过前瞻性学习与控制实现未来的最优控制
对未来的最优控制是人工智能的下一个前沿。当前解决该问题的方法通常基于强化学习（RL）。RL在数学上不同于监督学习，而监督学习是近期AI成就的主要驱动力。此外，RL通常在具有情节重置的平稳环境中运行，限制了其实用性。在此，我们将监督学习扩展到解决非平稳、无重置环境中的学习控制问题。利用这一称为“前瞻性学习与控制”（PLuC）的框架，我们证明在相当一般的假设下，经验风险最小化（ERM）渐近地达到贝叶斯最优策略。随后，我们考虑前瞻性学习与控制的一个具体实例：觅食，这是自然和人工智能体都相关的典型任务。我们说明，假设平稳性的现代RL算法在这些非平稳无重置环境中表现不佳。即使采用时间感知的修改，它们在简单的1维觅食基准测试中的收敛速度也比我们的前瞻性觅食智能体慢数个数量级。代码见：https://github.com/neurodata/procontrol。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Prospective Learning with Control (PLuC), a framework that extends supervised learning to address optimal control in non-stationary, reset-free environments, motivated by the limitations of reinforcement learning (RL) which assumes stationarity and episodic resets. The method proves that under general assumptions, empirical risk minimization (ERM) asymptotically achieves the Bayes optimal policy. In a 1-D foraging benchmark, the proposed prospective agents converge orders of magnitude faster than modern RL algorithms, even those with time-aware modifications, demonstrating superior performance in non-stationary settings.
该论文提出了前瞻性学习与控制（PLuC）框架，将监督学习扩展到非平稳、无重置环境中的最优控制问题，以克服强化学习（RL）依赖平稳性和回合重置的局限性。方法证明在一般假设下，经验风险最小化（ERM）渐近地达到贝叶斯最优策略。在1维觅食基准测试中，前瞻性代理的收敛速度比现代RL算法（包括时间感知改进版本）快数个数量级，展示了在非平稳环境中的优越性能。
Enhancing RL Generalizability in Robotics through SHAP Analysis of Algorithms and Hyperparameters
Authors: Lingxiao Kong, Cong Yang, Oya Deniz Beyan, Zeyd Boukhers
First: 2026-05-04T17:41:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T17:41:04+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 7 figures, accepted by ICPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite significant advances in Reinforcement Learning (RL), model performance remains highly sensitive to algorithm and hyperparameter configurations, while generalization gaps across environments complicate real-world deployment. Although prior work has studied RL generalization, the relative contribution of specific configurations to the generalization gap has not been quantitatively decomposed and systematically leveraged for configuration selection. To address this limitation, we propose an explainable framework that evaluates RL performance across robotic environments using SHapley Additive exPlanations (SHAP) to quantify configuration impacts. We establish a theoretical foundation connecting Shapley values to generalizability, empirically analyze configuration impact patterns, and introduce SHAP-guided configuration selection to enhance generalization. Our results reveal distinct patterns across algorithms and hyperparameters, with consistent configuration impacts across diverse tasks and environments. By applying these insights to configuration selection, we achieve improved RL generalizability and provide actionable guidance for practitioners.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过SHAP分析算法与超参数增强机器人强化学习泛化性
尽管强化学习取得了显著进展，模型性能仍对算法和超参数配置高度敏感，而跨环境的泛化差距则阻碍了实际部署。虽然已有研究探讨了强化学习的泛化性，但特定配置对泛化差距的相对贡献尚未被定量分解并系统性地用于配置选择。为解决这一局限，我们提出一个可解释框架，利用沙普利加性解释量化配置影响，评估机器人环境中的强化学习性能。我们建立了连接沙普利值与泛化性的理论基础，实证分析了配置影响模式，并引入SHAP引导的配置选择以增强泛化性。我们的结果揭示了算法与超参数的不同模式，且配置影响在多样任务与环境中保持一致。通过将这些见解应用于配置选择，我们实现了强化学习泛化性的提升，并为实践者提供了可操作的指导。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of poor generalization in Reinforcement Learning (RL) for robotics, where model performance is highly sensitive to algorithm and hyperparameter choices. The authors propose an explainable framework using SHAP (SHapley Additive exPlanations) to quantitatively decompose the impact of specific configurations on the generalization gap, establishing a theoretical link between Shapley values and generalizability. Through empirical analysis across diverse robotic environments, they identify distinct patterns in configuration impacts and introduce SHAP-guided configuration selection. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach improves RL generalizability, offering actionable guidance for practitioners.
该论文针对强化学习在机器人应用中泛化能力差的问题，指出模型性能对算法和超参数配置高度敏感。作者提出一个可解释框架，利用SHAP值量化不同配置对泛化差距的影响，建立了Shapley值与泛化性的理论联系。通过在多种机器人环境中的实证分析，他们识别出算法和超参数的不同影响模式，并引入基于SHAP的配置选择方法。实验结果表明，该方法有效提升了强化学习的泛化能力，为实践者提供了可操作的指导。
TOC-SR: Task-Optimal Compact diffusion for Image Super Resolution
Authors: Sowmya Vajrala, Akshay Bankar, Manjunath Arveti, Shreyas Pandith, Sravanth Kodavanti, Subhajit Sanyal, Amit Unde, Srinivas Soumitri Miriyala
First: 2026-05-04T16:06:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T16:06:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion models have recently demonstrated strong performance for image restoration tasks, including super-resolution. However, their large model size and iterative sampling procedures make them computationally expensive for practical deployment. In this work, we present TOC-SR, a framework for building efficient one-step super-resolution models by first discovering a compact diffusion backbone. Starting from a sixteen-channel latent diffusion model, we construct parameter-efficient surrogate blocks using feature-wise generative distillation and perform architecture discovery using epsilon-constrained Bayesian Optimization to minimize model complexity while preserving generative fidelity. The resulting compact diffusion backbone achieves a 6.6x reduction in parameters and a 2.8x reduction in GMACs compared to the expanded diffusion model. We then adapt this backbone for super-resolution and distill the diffusion process into a single-step generator. Experiments demonstrate that the proposed approach enables efficient super-resolution while maintaining strong reconstruction quality.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TOC-SR：面向图像超分辨率的任务最优紧凑扩散模型
扩散模型在图像超分辨率等恢复任务中展现出强大性能，但其庞大的模型规模和迭代采样过程导致实际部署时计算成本高昂。本文提出TOC-SR框架，通过首先发现紧凑扩散骨干网络来构建高效的单步超分辨率模型。从十六通道潜扩散模型出发，利用特征级生成蒸馏构建参数高效的替代模块，并采用ε约束贝叶斯优化进行架构发现，在保持生成保真度的同时最小化模型复杂度。与扩展扩散模型相比，所得紧凑扩散骨干网络参数量减少6.6倍，GMACs降低2.8倍。随后将该骨干网络适配至超分辨率任务，并将扩散过程蒸馏为单步生成器。实验表明，所提方法在保持强重建质量的同时实现了高效超分辨率。

Perceptual Flow Network for Visually Grounded Reasoning
Authors: Yangfu Li, Yuning Gong, Hongjian Zhan, Teng Li, Yuanhuiyi Lyu, Tianyi Chen, Qi Liu, Ziyuan Huang, Zhihang Zhong, Dandan Zheng, Yue Lu
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-05-04T15:31:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T15:31:11+00:00
Comments: 36 pages with 17 figures, Accepted at ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite the success of Large-Vision Language Models (LVLMs), general optimization objectives (e.g., standard MLE) fail to constrain visual trajectories, leading to language bias and hallucination. To mitigate this, current methods introduce geometric priors from visual experts as additional supervision. However, we observe that such supervision is typically suboptimal: it is biased toward geometric precision and offers limited reasoning utility. To bridge this gap, we propose Perceptual Flow Network (PFlowNet), which eschews rigid alignment with the expert priors and achieves interpretable yet more effective visual reasoning. Specifically, PFlowNet decouples perception from reasoning to establish a self-conditioned generation process. Based on this, it integrates multi-dimensional rewards with vicinal geometric shaping via variational reinforcement learning, thereby facilitating reasoning-oriented perceptual behaviors while preserving visual reliability. PFlowNet delivers a provable performance guarantee and competitive empirical results, particularly setting new SOTA records on V* Bench (90.6%) and MME-RealWorld-lite (67.0%).
中文标题/摘要
标题：感知流网络：面向视觉基础推理
尽管大型视觉语言模型（LVLMs）取得了成功，但通用优化目标（如标准MLE）无法约束视觉轨迹，导致语言偏差和幻觉。为缓解此问题，现有方法引入来自视觉专家的几何先验作为额外监督。然而，我们观察到这种监督通常次优：它偏向几何精度，且推理效用有限。为弥合这一差距，我们提出感知流网络（PFlowNet），它摒弃与专家先验的严格对齐，实现可解释且更有效的视觉推理。具体而言，PFlowNet将感知与推理解耦，建立自条件生成过程。在此基础上，通过变分强化学习整合多维奖励与邻域几何塑形，从而在保持视觉可靠性的同时促进面向推理的感知行为。PFlowNet提供了可证明的性能保证和有竞争力的实证结果，尤其在V* Bench（90.6%）和MME-RealWorld-lite（67.0%）上创下新的SOTA记录。
Summary / 总结
Large Vision-Language Models suffer from language bias and hallucination because standard maximum likelihood estimation fails to constrain visual reasoning trajectories. To address this, the authors propose Perceptual Flow Network (PFlowNet), which avoids rigid alignment with suboptimal geometric priors from visual experts. The method decouples perception from reasoning into a self-conditioned generation process and integrates multi-dimensional rewards with vicinal geometric shaping via variational reinforcement learning. PFlowNet achieves new state-of-the-art results on V* Bench (90.6%) and MME-RealWorld-lite (67.0%), demonstrating both provable performance guarantees and competitive empirical outcomes.
大型视觉语言模型因标准最大似然估计无法约束视觉推理轨迹，导致语言偏差和幻觉。为此，作者提出感知流网络（PFlowNet），避免与视觉专家提供的次优几何先验进行刚性对齐。该方法将感知与推理解耦为自条件生成过程，并通过变分强化学习整合多维奖励与邻域几何塑形。PFlowNet在V* Bench（90.6%）和MME-RealWorld-lite（67.0%）上取得新的最佳结果，兼具可证明的性能保证和竞争力的实证表现。
RAST-MoE-RL: A Regime-Aware Spatio-Temporal MoE Framework for Deep Reinforcement Learning in Ride-Hailing
Authors: Yuhan Tang, Kangxin Cui, Jung Ho Park, Yibo Zhao, Xuan Jiang, Haoze He, Jiangbo Yu, Haris Koutsopoulos, Jinhua Zhao
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2025-12-13T20:49:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T15:30:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Ride-hailing platforms face the challenge of balancing passenger waiting times with overall system efficiency under highly uncertain supply-demand conditions. Adaptive delayed matching, which controls the holding intervals for batched sets of requests and vehicles, reveals an inherent trade-off between matching and pickup delays. The resulting environment with temporally varying request arrival patterns and dynamic congestion calls for more expressive networks with sufficient capacity to capture their non-stationarity. To address the limitations of existing methods that rely on shallow encoders that cannot capture dynamic supply-demand patterns and congestion effects, we introduce the Regime-Aware Spatio-Temporal Mixture-of-Experts (RAST-MoE) framework, which formalizes adaptive delayed matching as a regime-aware Markov Decision Process and equips RL agents with a self-attention MoE encoder. Instead of relying on a single monolithic network, our design allows different experts to specialize automatically in varying operational conditions, improving representation capacity while maintaining per-sample computation efficiency. Despite its modest size of only 12M parameters, our framework consistently outperforms strong baselines. On real-world Uber trajectory data from San Francisco, it reduces average matching delay by 10%, and pickup delay by 15%. In addition, it demonstrates robustness to unseen demand regimes, stable training behavior without reward hacking, and expert specialization to different regimes. This study shows the strength of MoE-enhanced RL for large-scale decision-making tasks with complex spatiotemporal dynamics.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of balancing passenger waiting times and system efficiency in ride-hailing platforms under uncertain supply-demand conditions, where adaptive delayed matching involves a trade-off between matching and pickup delays. To overcome the limitations of existing methods with shallow encoders that fail to capture dynamic patterns and congestion, the authors propose the Regime-Aware Spatio-Temporal Mixture-of-Experts (RAST-MoE) framework, which formalizes the problem as a regime-aware Markov Decision Process and uses a self-attention MoE encoder to allow expert specialization under varying operational conditions. Despite having only 12 million parameters, the framework outperforms strong baselines on real-world Uber trajectory data from San Francisco, reducing average matching delay by 10% and pickup delay by 15%, while demonstrating robustness to unseen demand regimes and stable training without reward hacking.
该论文针对网约车平台在高度不确定的供需条件下平衡乘客等待时间与系统效率的挑战，其中自适应延迟匹配涉及匹配延迟与接驾延迟之间的固有权衡。为克服现有方法依赖浅层编码器、无法捕捉动态供需模式与拥堵效应的局限，作者提出了RAST-MoE框架，将自适应延迟匹配形式化为一个基于状态感知的马尔可夫决策过程，并采用自注意力混合专家编码器，使不同专家能够自动适应变化的运营条件。该框架仅含1200万参数，在旧金山真实Uber轨迹数据上持续优于强基线，将平均匹配延迟降低10%，接驾延迟降低15%，同时展现出对未见需求模式的鲁棒性、无奖励破解的稳定训练以及专家对不同状态的专业化分工。
Federated Reinforcement Learning for Efficient Mobile Crowdsensing under Incomplete Information
Authors: Sumedh J. Dongare, Patrick Weber, Andrea Ortiz, Walid Saad, Oliver Hinz, Anja Klein
First: 2026-05-04T15:13:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T15:13:16+00:00
Comments: This work has been submitted to the IEEE for possible publication
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Mobile crowdsensing (MCS) is a distributed sensing architecture that utilizes existing sensors on mobile units (MUs) to perform sensing tasks. A mobile crowdsensing platform (MCSP) publishes the sensing tasks and the MUs decide whether to participate in exchange for money. The MCS system is dynamic: the task requirements, the MUs' availability, and their available resources change over time. The MUs aim to find an efficient task participation strategy to maximize their income while the MCSP focuses on maximizing the number of completed tasks. As optimal strategies require perfect non-causal information about the MCS system, which is unavailable in realistic scenarios, the main challenge is to find an efficient task participation strategy for the MUs under incomplete information. To this end, a novel fully decentralized federated deep reinforcement learning algorithm, FDRL-PPO, is proposed. FDRL-PPO enables every MU to learn its own task participation strategy based on its experiences, available resources, and preferences, without relying on perfect non-causal information about the MCS system. To replenish their batteries, the MUs rely on energy harvesting. As a result, their available energy varies over time, leading to varying availability and fragmented learning experiences. To mitigate these challenges, the proposed approach leverages federated learning, enabling MUs to collaboratively improve their models without sharing private raw data like their own experiences. By exchanging only learned models, MUs collectively compensate for individual limitations, and find more scalable, robust, and efficient task participation strategies. Comprehensive evaluations on both synthetic and real-world datasets show that FDRL-PPO consistently outperforms benchmark algorithms in terms of task completion ratio, fairness in task completion, energy consumption, and number of conflicting proposals.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向不完全信息下高效移动群智感知的联邦强化学习
移动群智感知（MCS）是一种利用移动单元（MU）现有传感器执行感知任务的分布式感知架构。移动群智感知平台（MCSP）发布感知任务，MU决定是否参与以换取报酬。MCS系统具有动态性：任务需求、MU的可用性及其可用资源随时间变化。MU旨在寻找高效的任务参与策略以最大化收入，而MCSP则专注于最大化已完成任务数量。由于最优策略需要关于MCS系统的完美非因果信息，这在现实场景中不可得，主要挑战在于不完全信息下为MU寻找高效的任务参与策略。为此，提出了一种新颖的完全去中心化联邦深度强化学习算法FDRL-PPO。FDRL-PPO使每个MU能够基于自身经验、可用资源和偏好学习其任务参与策略，无需依赖关于MCS系统的完美非因果信息。MU依靠能量收集来补充电池，因此其可用能量随时间变化，导致可用性波动和学习经验碎片化。为缓解这些挑战，所提方法利用联邦学习，使MU能够在不共享私有原始数据（如自身经验）的情况下协作改进模型。通过仅交换学习到的模型，MU共同弥补个体局限性，并找到更具可扩展性、鲁棒性和高效性的任务参与策略。在合成数据集和真实数据集上的全面评估表明，FDRL-PPO在任务完成率、任务完成公平性、能耗和冲突提案数量方面始终优于基准算法。

The authors propose a fully decentralized federated deep reinforcement learning algorithm, FDRL-PPO, which enables each MU to learn its own participation strategy based on local experiences, resources, and preferences, while leveraging federated learning to collaboratively improve models without sharing raw data. Comprehensive evaluations on synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that FDRL-PPO consistently outperforms benchmark algorithms in task completion ratio, fairness, energy consumption, and reduction of conflicting proposals.
本文针对移动群智感知中信息不完全条件下的高效任务参与问题展开研究，其中移动单元需在缺乏系统完美先验知识的情况下优化自身策略。作者提出了一种完全去中心化的联邦深度强化学习算法FDRL-PPO，使每个移动单元能基于本地经验、资源和偏好学习个性化参与策略，同时通过联邦学习在不共享原始数据的前提下协作提升模型性能。在合成数据集和真实数据集上的综合评估表明，FDRL-PPO在任务完成率、公平性、能耗以及冲突提案数量等指标上均持续优于基准算法。
Caliper-in-the-Loop: Black-Box Optimization for Hyperledger Fabric Performance Tuning
Authors: Yash Madhwal, Arseny Bolotnikov, Mark Prikhno, Irina Lebedeva, Ivan Laishevskiy, Vladimir Gorgadze, Artem Barger, Yury Yanovich
First: 2026-05-04T15:04:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T15:04:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Hyperledger Fabric performance depends on many interacting configuration parameters, making manual tuning difficult. We study automated throughput tuning by treating benchmarking as a noisy black-box optimization problem and applying Bayesian optimization (BO) with dimensionality reduction (DR). We implement an end-to-end Caliper-in-the-loop pipeline that deploys candidate configurations, benchmarks them, and updates the optimizer from observed throughput. The search space, derived from Fabric configuration files, has 317 dimensions. In a cloud testbed, we evaluate 16 BO+DR variants and a random-search baseline. The best method, DYCORS-PCA, achieves a 12% TPS improvement relative to the first evaluated configuration, while MPI-REMBO achieves 9%. These results suggest that BO with DR is a practical approach for high-dimensional Hyperledger Fabric tuning, while also highlighting the role of measurement noise in interpreting gains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：卡尺在环：面向Hyperledger Fabric性能调优的黑盒优化
Hyperledger Fabric的性能依赖于众多相互作用的配置参数，使得手动调优困难重重。我们通过将基准测试视为带噪声的黑盒优化问题，并应用结合降维的贝叶斯优化，研究自动化吞吐量调优。我们实现了一个端到端的卡尺在环流水线，该流水线部署候选配置、进行基准测试，并根据观测到的吞吐量更新优化器。从Fabric配置文件中导出的搜索空间包含317个维度。在云测试平台上，我们评估了16种贝叶斯优化加降维变体以及一个随机搜索基线。最佳方法DYCORS-PCA相较于首个评估配置实现了12%的TPS提升，而MPI-REMBO实现了9%的提升。这些结果表明，结合降维的贝叶斯优化是面向高维Hyperledger Fabric调优的实用方法，同时也凸显了测量噪声在解释增益中的作用。
Summary / 总结

Q-RAG: Long Context Multi-step Retrieval via Value-based Embedder Training
Authors: Artyom Sorokin, Nazar Buzun, Alexander Anokhin, Oleg Inozemcev, Egor Vedernikov, Petr Anokhin, Mikhail Burtsev, Trushkov Alexey, Yin Wenshuai, Evgeny Burnaev
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-11-10T17:31:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T15:02:13+00:00
Comments: Published as a conference paper at ICLR 2026. Code is available at https://github.com/griver/Q-RAG
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) methods enhance LLM performance by efficiently filtering relevant context for LLMs, reducing hallucinations and inference cost. However, most existing RAG methods focus on single-step retrieval, which is often insufficient for answering complex questions that require multi-step search. Recently, multi-step retrieval approaches have emerged, typically involving the fine-tuning of small LLMs to perform multi-step retrieval. This type of fine-tuning is highly resource-intensive and does not enable the use of larger LLMs. In this work, we propose Q-RAG, a novel approach that fine-tunes the Embedder model for multi-step retrieval using reinforcement learning (RL). Q-RAG offers a competitive, resource-efficient alternative to existing multi-step retrieval methods for open-domain question answering and achieves state-of-the-art results on the popular long-context benchmarks BabiLong and RULER for contexts up to 10M tokens. Code is available at https://github.com/griver/Q-RAG
中文标题/摘要
标题：Q-RAG：基于价值嵌入器训练的长上下文多步检索
检索增强生成（RAG）方法通过高效过滤相关上下文来提升大语言模型（LLM）性能，减少幻觉和推理成本。然而，现有大多数RAG方法专注于单步检索，这通常不足以回答需要多步搜索的复杂问题。近期，多步检索方法逐渐兴起，通常涉及微调小型LLM以执行多步检索。这种微调方式资源消耗大，且无法使用更大的LLM。在本工作中，我们提出Q-RAG，一种通过强化学习（RL）微调嵌入器模型以实现多步检索的新方法。Q-RAG为开放域问答提供了具有竞争力且资源高效的替代方案，并在流行的长上下文基准BabiLong和RULER上（上下文长度达1000万token）取得了最先进的结果。代码已开源：https://github.com/griver/Q-RAG
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Q-RAG, a method for multi-step retrieval in long-context question answering that addresses the limitations of existing single-step retrieval approaches. The motivation is to efficiently handle complex queries requiring sequential information gathering without the high resource cost of fine-tuning large language models. The method fine-tunes an embedder model using reinforcement learning to perform value-based multi-step retrieval, enabling iterative context selection. Experimental results demonstrate state-of-the-art performance on the BabiLong and RULER benchmarks for contexts up to 10 million tokens, showing competitive and resource-efficient improvements over existing multi-step retrieval techniques.

AcademiClaw: When Students Set Challenges for AI Agents
Authors: Junjie Yu, Pengrui Lu, Weiye Si, Hongliang Lu, Jiabao Wu, Kaiwen Tao, Kun Wang, Lingyu Yang, Qiran Zhang, Xiuting Guo, Xuanyu Wang, Yang Wang, Yanjie Wang, Yi Yang, Zijian Hu, Ziyi Yang, Zonghan Zhou, Binghao Qiang, Borui Zhang, Chenning Li, Enchang Zhang, Feifan Chen, Feng Jian, Fengyin Sun, Hao Qiu, Hao Zheng, Haoran Zhu, Hongyu Liu, Jianbin Deng, Jiaxin Song, Jiaying Chi, Jiayou Shi, Jie Fang, Jinghui Zhong, Jingyu Zhou, Jinze Li, Junfeng Yi, Junyan Yu, Junzhi Xue, Ni Song, Pengyi Chen, Qi Chen, Quansheng Li, Rui Tao, Shenghai Gong, Shenhang Lu, Tianqi Shen, Tianxiang Zhu, Tiehan Kang, Tingyu Li, Wendi Wu, Xiao Shen, Xiao Zhou, Xiaotao Zhang, Xinrong Li, Xuankun Yang, Xun Zhang, Yan Li, Ye Lu, Yi Wang, Yibo Zhou, Yichi Zhang, Yihao Sun, Yijun Huang, Yixin Zhu, Yixuan Wu, Yuchen Sun, Yue Wu, Yuheng Sun, Yukun Li, Yutian Tu, Yuxuan Qin, Yuzhuo Wu, Zeyu Li, Zhengyu Lou, Zhenning Ran, Zizhu He, Pengfei Liu
First: 2026-05-04T14:40:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T14:40:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Benchmarks within the OpenClaw ecosystem have thus far evaluated exclusively assistant-level tasks, leaving the academic-level capabilities of OpenClaw largely unexamined. We introduce AcademiClaw, a bilingual benchmark of 80 complex, long-horizon tasks sourced directly from university students' real academic workflows -- homework, research projects, competitions, and personal projects -- that they found current AI agents unable to solve effectively. Curated from 230 student-submitted candidates through rigorous expert review, the final task set spans 25+ professional domains, ranging from olympiad-level mathematics and linguistics problems to GPU-intensive reinforcement learning and full-stack system debugging, with 16 tasks requiring CUDA GPU execution. Each task executes in an isolated Docker sandbox and is scored on task completion by multi-dimensional rubrics combining six complementary techniques, with an independent five-category safety audit providing additional behavioral analysis. Experiments on six frontier models show that even the best achieves only a 55\% pass rate. Further analysis uncovers sharp capability boundaries across task domains, divergent behavioral strategies among models, and a disconnect between token consumption and output quality, providing fine-grained diagnostic signals beyond what aggregate metrics reveal. We hope that AcademiClaw and its open-sourced data and code can serve as a useful resource for the OpenClaw community, driving progress toward agents that are more capable and versatile across the full breadth of real-world academic demands. All data and code are available at https://github.com/GAIR-NLP/AcademiClaw.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AcademiClaw：当学生为AI智能体设置挑战
OpenClaw生态系统中的基准测试迄今仅评估了助手级别的任务，使得OpenClaw的学术级能力在很大程度上未被检验。我们引入了AcademiClaw，这是一个包含80个复杂、长周期任务的双语基准测试，这些任务直接来源于大学生真实的学术工作流程——作业、研究项目、竞赛和个人项目——他们发现当前的AI智能体无法有效解决这些问题。经过严格专家评审，从230个学生提交的候选任务中筛选出最终任务集，涵盖25个以上专业领域，从奥林匹克级别的数学和语言学问题到GPU密集型强化学习和全栈系统调试，其中16个任务需要CUDA GPU执行。每个任务在隔离的Docker沙箱中执行，并通过结合六种互补技术的多维评分标准对任务完成情况进行评分，同时独立的五类安全审计提供额外的行为分析。对六个前沿模型的实验表明，即使是最佳模型也仅达到55%的通过率。进一步分析揭示了任务领域间尖锐的能力边界、模型间不同的行为策略以及令牌消耗与输出质量之间的脱节，提供了超越聚合指标所揭示的细粒度诊断信号。我们希望AcademiClaw及其开源数据和代码能够为OpenClaw社区提供有用资源，推动智能体在真实世界学术需求的广泛范围内变得更加有能力和多才多艺。所有数据和代码可在https://github.com/GAIR-NLP/AcademiClaw获取。

Gradient-Gated DPO: Stabilizing Preference Optimization in Language Models
Authors: Inoussa Mouiche
First: 2026-05-04T14:15:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T14:15:24+00:00
Comments: 21 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Preference optimization has become a central paradigm for aligning large language models with human feedback. Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) simplifies reinforcement learning from human feedback by directly optimizing pairwise preferences, removing the need for reward modeling and policy optimization. However, recent work shows that DPO exhibits a squeezing effect, where negative gradients applied to rejected responses concentrate probability mass on high-confidence predictions while suppressing alternative responses. This phenomenon arises even in simple softmax models and can lead to systematic probability collapse during training. We introduce Gradient-Gated Preference Optimization (Gate-DPO), a method that stabilizes training by modulating rejected gradients according to the model's probability geometry. When updates target extremely low-probability responses, the gate attenuates harmful gradients while preserving standard optimization behavior. Gate-DPO addresses this optimization pathology without modifying the underlying preference objective and is complementary to existing methods such as extended SFT, IPO, and Cal-DPO. Experiments across multiple architectures and preference datasets show that Gate-DPO consistently reduces squeezing and improves chosen-response likelihood. Mass-dynamics analysis further reveals healthier optimization behavior, with improved preferred responses and reduced suppression of the overall distribution. Notably, smaller gated models can exhibit stronger chosen-response improvements than larger ungated models, suggesting that controlling gradient dynamics, rather than scale alone, is key to stable and efficient alignment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：梯度门控DPO：稳定语言模型中的偏好优化
偏好优化已成为将大型语言模型与人类反馈对齐的核心范式。直接偏好优化（DPO）通过直接优化成对偏好简化了从人类反馈中进行的强化学习，无需奖励建模和策略优化。然而，近期研究表明DPO存在挤压效应，即对拒绝响应施加的负梯度将概率质量集中在高置信度预测上，同时抑制替代响应。即使在简单的softmax模型中也会出现此现象，并可能导致训练过程中系统性的概率坍缩。我们提出梯度门控偏好优化（Gate-DPO），该方法通过根据模型的概率几何调节拒绝梯度来稳定训练。当更新针对极低概率响应时，门控机制会衰减有害梯度，同时保留标准优化行为。Gate-DPO在不修改底层偏好目标的情况下解决了这一优化病理问题，并与扩展SFT、IPO和Cal-DPO等现有方法互补。跨多种架构和偏好数据集的实验表明，Gate-DPO持续减少挤压效应并提高选择响应的似然性。质量动态分析进一步揭示了更健康的优化行为，改善了偏好响应并减少了对整体分布的抑制。值得注意的是，较小的门控模型在提升选择响应方面可能优于较大的非门控模型，这表明控制梯度动态（而非仅依赖规模）是实现稳定高效对齐的关键。
Summary / 总结
The paper identifies a squeezing effect in Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) for aligning language models, where negative gradients on rejected responses cause probability mass to collapse onto high-confidence predictions, suppressing alternatives. To address this, the authors propose Gradient-Gated Preference Optimization (Gate-DPO), which modulates rejected gradients based on the model's probability geometry, attenuating harmful updates for low-probability responses while preserving standard behavior. Experiments across multiple architectures and datasets show that Gate-DPO consistently reduces squeezing, improves chosen-response likelihood, and enables smaller gated models to outperform larger ungated ones, highlighting the importance of controlling gradient dynamics over model scale for stable alignment.
该论文发现直接偏好优化（DPO）在对齐语言模型时存在挤压效应，即对拒绝响应的负梯度会导致概率质量集中在高置信度预测上，抑制其他响应。为此，作者提出梯度门控偏好优化（Gate-DPO），根据模型的概率几何调节拒绝梯度，在针对低概率响应时减弱有害更新，同时保持标准优化行为。在多种架构和偏好数据集上的实验表明，Gate-DPO持续减少挤压效应，提升选择响应的似然性，并且较小的门控模型能超越较大的非门控模型，凸显了控制梯度动力学而非单纯扩大模型规模对于稳定对齐的关键作用。
SCALER:Synthetic Scalable Adaptive Learning Environment for Reasoning
Authors: Caijun Xu, Changyi Xiao, Zhongyuan Peng, Xinrun Wang, Yixin Cao
First: 2026-01-08T10:42:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T13:55:24+00:00
Comments: 23 pages,5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) offers a principled way to enhance the reasoning capabilities of large language models, yet its effectiveness hinges on training signals that remain informative as models evolve. In practice, RL progress often slows when task difficulty becomes poorly aligned with model capability, or when training is dominated by a narrow set of recurring problem patterns. To jointly address these issues, we propose SCALER (Synthetic sCalable Adaptive Learning Environment for Reasoning), a framework that sustains effective learning signals through adaptive environment design. SCALER introduces a scalable synthesis pipeline that converts real-world programming problems into verifiable reasoning environments with controllable difficulty and unbounded instance generation, enabling RL training beyond finite datasets while preserving strong correctness guarantees. Building on this, SCALER further employs an adaptive multi-environment RL strategy that dynamically adjusts instance difficulty and curates the active set of environments to track the model's capability frontier and maintain distributional diversity. This co-adaptation prevents reward sparsity, mitigates overfitting to narrow task patterns, and supports sustained improvement throughout training. Extensive experiments show that SCALER consistently outperforms dataset-based RL baselines across diverse reasoning benchmarks and exhibits more stable, long-horizon training dynamics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SCALER：面向推理的可扩展合成自适应学习环境
强化学习（RL）为提升大语言模型的推理能力提供了一种原则性方法，但其有效性依赖于随模型进化仍保持信息量的训练信号。实践中，当任务难度与模型能力不匹配，或训练被少量重复问题模式主导时，RL进展常会放缓。为联合解决这些问题，我们提出SCALER（面向推理的可扩展合成自适应学习环境），一种通过自适应环境设计维持有效学习信号的框架。SCALER引入可扩展的合成流水线，将现实编程问题转化为难度可控、实例生成无界的可验证推理环境，使RL训练超越有限数据集的同时保持强正确性保证。在此基础上，SCALER进一步采用自适应多环境RL策略，动态调整实例难度并精选活跃环境集，以追踪模型能力边界并维持分布多样性。这种协同适应可防止奖励稀疏、缓解对狭窄任务模式的过拟合，并支持训练过程中的持续改进。大量实验表明，SCALER在多种推理基准上持续优于基于数据集的RL基线，并展现出更稳定、更长周期的训练动态。
Summary / 总结
