本文基于PRISMA指南对深度强化学习中预训练知识复用的实证研究进行了系统性综述，其动机在于DRL方法的高样本成本和弱迁移能力。作者从主要数据库中筛选了570条独特记录，并分析了15项符合条件的研究，涵盖源-目标相似性、复用模型多样性及比较公平性三个因素。主要结果表明，正面结果集中在具有显著结构相似性或显式门控机制的设置中，集成和联邦聚合的证据虽有前景但稀疏，且计算匹配的比较罕见，削弱了效率提升的主张。
Reinforcement Learning Trained Observer Control for Bearings-Only Tracking
Authors: Branko Ristic, Sanjeev Arulampalam
First: 2026-05-04T00:55:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T00:55:14+00:00
Comments: 7 pages, 2 figures, 3 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper develops a deep reinforcement learning based observer control policy for autonomous bearings-only tracking of a moving target. The observer manoeuvre problem is formulated as a belief Markov decision process, where the belief state is represented by the posterior of a cubature Kalman filter (CKF). The reward function is designed to address two conflicting objectives: minimising the absolute target position estimation error (Euclidean distance) and maintaining CKF estimation consistency (Mahalanobis distance). The reward is formulated as a geometric interpolation between the two objectives on the Pareto front, parametrised by a weighting factor $β\in [0,1]$. The policy is implemented as a deep Q-network (DQN) trained over 50,000 episodes. Performance is evaluated over 5,000 Monte Carlo episodes and compared against two baselines: the perpendicular-to-bearing heuristic and the D-optimal Fisher information maximisation criterion. The results show that the DQN policy at $β= 0.7$ achieves the best trade-off between accuracy and robustness: it matches the information-theoretic baseline on mean tracking accuracy while reducing the worst-case error by nearly a factor of ten, owing to the implicit filter-consistency regularisation provided by the Mahalanobis term in the reward.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于强化学习的纯方位跟踪观测器控制
本文提出了一种基于深度强化学习的观测器控制策略，用于对移动目标进行自主纯方位跟踪。观测器机动问题被建模为信念马尔可夫决策过程，其中信念状态由容积卡尔曼滤波的后验表示。奖励函数旨在解决两个相互冲突的目标：最小化目标位置绝对估计误差（欧氏距离）和保持CKF估计一致性（马氏距离）。奖励被构造为帕累托前沿上两个目标之间的几何插值，由权重因子β∈[0,1]参数化。该策略通过深度Q网络实现，并在50,000个回合上训练。性能在5,000次蒙特卡洛回合上评估，并与两个基线进行比较：垂直于方位启发式和D-最优Fisher信息最大化准则。结果表明，β=0.7时的DQN策略在精度和鲁棒性之间实现了最佳权衡：它在平均跟踪精度上与信息论基线相当，同时将最坏情况误差降低了近一个数量级，这归功于奖励中马氏项提供的隐式滤波一致性正则化。
Summary / 总结
This paper proposes a deep reinforcement learning based observer control policy for autonomous bearings-only tracking of a moving target. The observer maneuver problem is formulated as a belief Markov decision process, where the belief state is represented by the posterior of a cubature Kalman filter (CKF), and the reward function is designed as a geometric interpolation between minimizing Euclidean distance for accuracy and maintaining Mahalanobis distance for filter consistency, parametrized by a weighting factor β. The policy is implemented as a deep Q-network (DQN) trained over 50,000 episodes and evaluated over 5,000 Monte Carlo episodes, showing that at β=0.7, the DQN policy achieves the best trade-off: it matches the D-optimal Fisher information maximization baseline on mean tracking accuracy while reducing the worst-case error by nearly a factor of ten due to the implicit filter-consistency regularization from the Mahalanobis term.
本文提出了一种基于深度强化学习的观测器控制策略，用于对移动目标进行自主纯方位跟踪。观测器机动问题被建模为信念马尔可夫决策过程，其中信念状态由容积卡尔曼滤波的后验表示，奖励函数设计为最小化欧氏距离（精度）与保持马氏距离（滤波一致性）之间的几何插值，由权重因子β参数化。该策略通过深度Q网络实现，经过50000个回合训练，并在5000次蒙特卡洛回合中评估，结果表明在β=0.7时，DQN策略实现了最佳权衡：它在平均跟踪精度上与基于D-最优费舍尔信息最大化的基线相当，同时由于奖励中马氏距离项提供的隐式滤波一致性正则化，将最差情况误差降低了近十倍。
Control Reinforcement Learning: Interpretable Token-Level Steering of LLMs via Sparse Autoencoder Features
Authors: Seonglae Cho, Zekun Wu, Adriano Koshiyama
First: 2026-02-11T02:28:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-03T22:52:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) decompose language model activations into interpretable features, but existing methods reveal only which features activate, not which change model outputs when amplified. We introduce Control Reinforcement Learning (CRL), which trains a policy to select SAE features for steering at each token, producing interpretable intervention logs: the learned policy identifies features that change model outputs when amplified. Adaptive Feature Masking encourages diverse feature discovery while preserving singlefeature interpretability. The framework yields new analysis capabilities: branch point tracking locates tokens where feature choice determines output correctness; critic trajectory analysis separates policy limitations from value estimation errors; layer-wise comparison reveals syntactic features in early layers and semantic features in later layers. On Gemma 2 2B across MMLU, BBQ, GSM8K, HarmBench, and XSTest, CRL achieves improvements while providing per-token intervention logs. These results establish learned feature steering as a mechanistic interpretability tool that complements static feature analysis with dynamic intervention probes
中文标题/摘要
标题：控制强化学习：通过稀疏自编码器特征实现大语言模型的可解释词元级引导
稀疏自编码器将语言模型激活分解为可解释特征，但现有方法仅揭示哪些特征被激活，而非哪些特征在放大时能改变模型输出。我们提出控制强化学习，训练策略为每个词元选择用于引导的稀疏自编码器特征，生成可解释的干预日志：学习到的策略能识别出放大时改变模型输出的特征。自适应特征掩码在保持单特征可解释性的同时促进多样化特征发现。该框架带来新的分析能力：分支点追踪定位特征选择决定输出正确性的词元；评论家轨迹分析分离策略局限与价值估计误差；逐层比较揭示早期层的句法特征与后期层的语义特征。在Gemma 2 2B模型上，针对MMLU、BBQ、GSM8K、HarmBench和XSTest基准测试，控制强化学习在提供逐词元干预日志的同时实现了性能提升。这些结果确立了学习式特征引导作为一种机制可解释性工具，通过动态干预探针补充静态特征分析。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Control Reinforcement Learning (CRL), a method for interpretable token-level steering of large language models using sparse autoencoder (SAE) features. The motivation is that existing SAE-based approaches only identify which features activate but not which ones causally affect model outputs when amplified. CRL trains a policy via reinforcement learning to select SAE features for steering at each token, producing interpretable intervention logs. Adaptive Feature Masking is employed to encourage diverse feature discovery while preserving single-feature interpretability. The framework enables new analysis capabilities such as branch point tracking, critic trajectory analysis, and layer-wise comparison. Experiments on Gemma 2 2B across MMLU, BBQ, GSM8K, HarmBench, and XSTest show that CRL achieves performance improvements while providing per-token intervention logs, establishing learned feature steering as a dynamic mechanistic interpretability tool.
该论文提出了控制强化学习（CRL），一种通过稀疏自编码器（SAE）特征对大型语言模型进行可解释的逐词级引导的方法。其动机在于现有SAE方法仅能识别哪些特征被激活，而无法确定哪些特征在被放大时会改变模型输出。CRL通过强化学习训练一个策略，在每个词元上选择SAE特征进行引导，并生成可解释的干预日志。自适应特征掩码技术用于促进多样化的特征发现，同时保持单特征的可解释性。该框架支持分支点追踪、评论家轨迹分析和层间比较等新分析能力。在Gemma 2 2B模型上，针对MMLU、BBQ、GSM8K、HarmBench和XSTest数据集的实验表明，CRL在提升性能的同时提供了逐词元干预日志，从而将学习到的特征引导确立为一种动态的机制可解释性工具。
Coopetition-Gym v1: A Formally Grounded Platform for Mixed-Motive Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning under Strategic Coopetition
Authors: Vik Pant, Eric Yu
First: 2026-05-03T21:14:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-03T21:14:06+00:00
Comments: 82 pages, 14 figures, 9 tables, 51 references. AI-track technical report companion to the four-paper foundational series; should be read with arXiv:2510.18802, arXiv:2510.24909, arXiv:2601.16237, and arXiv:2604.01240. Reproducibility package and source code: https://github.com/vikpant/strategic-coopetition. Datasets released under CC-BY-4.0 at https://huggingface.co/vikpant
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
We present Coopetition-Gym v1, a benchmark platform for mixed-motive multi-agent reinforcement learning under strategic coopetition. The platform comprises twenty environments organized into four mechanism classes that correspond to four foundational technical reports: interdependence and complementarity (arXiv:2510.18802), trust and reputation dynamics (arXiv:2510.24909), collective action and loyalty (arXiv:2601.16237), and sequential interaction and reciprocity (arXiv:2604.01240). Each environment carries a closed-form payoff structure and a calibrated interdependence matrix derived from the corresponding report. Every environment exposes a parameterized reward layer configurable across three structurally distinct modes (private, integrated, cooperative). This separation of payoff from reward enables reward-type ablation, the platform's principal methodological apparatus. Four of the twenty environments are calibrated against historically documented coopetitive relationships and reproduce their outcomes at 98.3, 81.7, 86.7, and 87.3 percent on the validation rubric (Samsung-Sony LCD, Renault-Nissan Alliance, Apache HTTP Server, Apple iOS App Store). The platform exposes Gymnasium, PettingZoo Parallel, and PettingZoo AEC interfaces and ships 126 reference algorithms: 16 learning algorithms, 7 game-theoretic oracles, 2 heuristic baselines, and 101 constant-action policies. A reference experimental study trained the 16 learning algorithms on every environment under every reward configuration with seven random seeds, producing a 25,708-run training corpus and a 1,116-run behavioral audit corpus, both released under CC-BY-4.0 with Croissant 1.0 metadata. Coopetition-Gym v1 is the first platform to combine continuous-action mixed-motive environments, parameterized reward mutuality, calibrated interdependence coefficients, game-theoretic oracle baselines, and validated case studies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Coopetition-Gym v1：面向战略竞合下混合动机多智能体强化学习的正式化基准平台
我们提出Coopetition-Gym v1，一个面向战略竞合下混合动机多智能体强化学习的基准平台。该平台包含二十个环境，分为四个机制类别，对应四份基础技术报告：相互依赖与互补性（arXiv:2510.18802）、信任与声誉动态（arXiv:2510.24909）、集体行动与忠诚度（arXiv:2601.16237）、以及序列互动与互惠性（arXiv:2604.01240）。每个环境具有封闭形式的收益结构，以及从相应报告推导出的校准相互依赖矩阵。 每个环境暴露一个参数化奖励层，可在三种结构不同的模式（私有、集成、合作）下配置。这种收益与奖励的分离实现了奖励类型消融，即平台的主要方法论工具。二十个环境中有四个根据历史上记录的竞合关系进行校准，并在验证标准下以98.3%、81.7%、86.7%和87.3%的准确率复现其结果（三星-索尼LCD、雷诺-日产联盟、Apache HTTP服务器、苹果iOS应用商店）。 该平台提供Gymnasium、PettingZoo Parallel和PettingZoo AEC接口，并包含126个参考算法：16个学习算法、7个博弈论预言机、2个启发式基线以及101个恒定动作策略。一项参考实验研究在每种奖励配置下使用七个随机种子对每个环境训练了16个学习算法，生成了25,708次运行的训练语料库和1,116次运行的行为审计语料库，两者均以CC-BY-4.0许可发布，并附带Croissant 1.0元数据。Coopetition-Gym v1是首个结合连续动作混合动机环境、参数化奖励互惠性、校准相互依赖系数、博弈论预言机基线和验证案例研究的平台。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Coopetition-Gym v1, a benchmark platform for mixed-motive multi-agent reinforcement learning under strategic coopetition, motivated by the need for a formally grounded environment to study interactions involving both competition and cooperation. The platform includes twenty environments across four mechanism classes, each with closed-form payoff structures and calibrated interdependence matrices, and features a parameterized reward layer with three modes to enable reward-type ablation. Experimental results show that four environments calibrated against historical coopetitive relationships reproduce outcomes at 98.3%, 81.7%, 86.7%, and 87.3% accuracy, and a reference study with 16 learning algorithms across all configurations produced a 25,708-run training corpus and a 1,116-run behavioral audit corpus, establishing the platform as the first to combine continuous-action mixed-motive environments, parameterized reward mutuality, and validated case studies.
该论文介绍了Coopetition-Gym v1，一个用于战略竞合下混合动机多智能体强化学习的基准平台，其动机源于对形式化环境的需求，以研究同时涉及竞争与合作的行为。平台包含二十个环境，分为四个机制类别，每个环境具有闭式收益结构和校准的相互依赖矩阵，并设有三种模式的参数化奖励层以支持奖励类型消融实验。实验结果表明，四个基于历史竞合关系校准的环境在验证标准下分别达到98.3%、81.7%、86.7%和87.3%的复现准确率，而一项参考研究使用16种学习算法在所有配置下训练，生成了25,708次训练语料库和1,116次行为审计语料库，使该平台成为首个结合连续动作混合动机环境、参数化奖励互惠性和验证案例研究的平台。
Rationality Measurement and Theory for Reinforcement Learning Agents
Authors: Kejiang Qian, Amos Storkey, Fengxiang He
First: 2026-02-04T16:41:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-03T21:08:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
This paper proposes a suite of rationality measures and associated theory for reinforcement learning agents, a property increasingly critical yet rarely explored. We define an action in deployment to be perfectly rational if it maximises the hidden true value function in the steepest direction. The expected value discrepancy of a policy's actions against their rational counterparts, culminating over the trajectory in deployment, is defined to be expected rational risk; an empirical average version in training is also defined. Their difference, termed as rational risk gap, is decomposed into (1) an extrinsic component caused by environment shifts between training and deployment, and (2) an intrinsic one due to the algorithm's generalisability in a dynamic environment. They are upper bounded by, respectively, (1) the $1$-Wasserstein distance between transition kernels and initial state distributions in training and deployment, and (2) the empirical Rademacher complexity of the value function class. Our theory suggests hypotheses on the benefits from regularisers (including layer normalisation, $\ell_2$ regularisation, and weight normalisation) and domain randomisation, as well as the harm from environment shifts. Experiments are in full agreement with these hypotheses. The code is available at https://github.com/EVIEHub/Rationality.
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces a formal framework for measuring rationality in reinforcement learning agents, motivated by the need to understand and quantify how well an agent's actions align with optimal decision-making under hidden true value functions. The method defines perfect rationality as actions that maximize the true value in the steepest direction, and proposes expected rational risk to capture the discrepancy between a policy's actions and rational ones during deployment, along with a training-time empirical version. The rational risk gap is decomposed into extrinsic and intrinsic components, bounded by the 1-Wasserstein distance and empirical Rademacher complexity, respectively. Experiments validate theoretical hypotheses that regularizers like layer normalization and domain randomization improve rationality, while environment shifts harm it.
本文提出了一套用于强化学习智能体的理性度量框架及理论，旨在解决智能体行为与最优决策一致性的量化问题，该性质虽日益重要却鲜有探索。方法将完美理性定义为在隐藏真实价值函数最陡方向上最大化收益的动作，并定义了期望理性风险以衡量策略动作与理性动作在部署中的差异，同时给出了训练时的经验版本。理性风险缺口被分解为外在成分（由训练与部署环境变化引起）和内在成分（由算法在动态环境中的泛化能力决定），分别由1-Wasserstein距离和经验Rademacher复杂度上界约束。实验完全支持理论假设，即层归一化、L2正则化等正则化项和域随机化能提升理性，而环境变化则有害。代码已开源。
Optimization of CV-QKD Under Practical Constraints
Authors: Svitlana Matsenko, Amirhossein Ghazisaeidi, Marcin Jarzyna, Konrad Banaszek, Darko Zibar
First: 2026-05-03T20:26:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-03T20:26:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Using reinforcement learning, we optimize for practical hardware constraints, including limited FIR filter taps at the transmitter and receiver, mean photon number and finite DAC/ADC resolution. Under these realistic conditions, the proposed approach achieves significant performance improvements.
中文标题/摘要
标题：实际约束下的连续变量量子密钥分发优化
利用强化学习，我们针对实际硬件约束进行优化，包括发射机和接收机有限FIR滤波器抽头、平均光子数以及有限数模/模数转换器分辨率。在这些现实条件下，所提出的方法实现了显著的性能提升。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of optimizing continuous-variable quantum key distribution (CV-QKD) under practical hardware constraints, such as limited finite impulse response (FIR) filter taps, mean photon number, and finite DAC/ADC resolution. The authors propose a reinforcement learning-based method to adaptively tune system parameters for improved performance. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed approach achieves significant performance improvements under these realistic conditions.
本文针对连续变量量子密钥分发（CV-QKD）在实际硬件约束下的优化问题，包括有限FIR滤波器抽头、平均光子数以及有限DAC/ADC分辨率等限制。作者提出了一种基于强化学习的方法，通过自适应调整系统参数来提升性能。实验结果表明，该方法在这些现实条件下实现了显著的性能提升。
